name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Guestroom (Double bed)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:14 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:The hotel is in a great location, right by Yunlong Lake, and it is convenient for travel. It is very quiet at night. There are many big restaurants on Ruyi Road. If you want to eat local specialties, you can go to the old houses in Hubin Village.
The hotel service is even better. The service staff in the entire hotel are super enthusiastic. You can feel the enthusiasm from the heart when you meet and greet. The hotel concierge is also very enthusiastic, helping to put luggage and help to open and close the car door. In short, the service is good.
Speaking of breakfast, the hotel has prepared various Xuzhou breakfasts, spicy soup, fried buns, Xuzhou rice noodles, beef soup, and Luomo for tourists to taste the characteristics of Xuzhou. In short, it saves the time of running around to find special breakfasts. As long as you stay in the hotel, you can taste the characteristics of Xuzhou. This is really great.
The only drawback is that the room is a bit hot, and the balcony door is opened for ventilation without a screen door. Everything else is very good. I will recommend it to my friends and will stay in Kaiyuan again when I go to Xuzhou in the future.
